Let \(F_{\text{GT}}(t,P)\) be the fixed ground-truth function. From the provided GT numerical expression, note:

- **GT has no \(t\) dependence at all**. So any candidate that depends on \(t\) must have its \(t\)-dependent part forced to zero (by setting some candidate constants to 0), otherwise it cannot match for all \(t\).
- GT is a **sum of three \(P\)-only terms**:
  1) a **cubic polynomial in \(P\)**: \(0.1387\cdot(-1+P/8.0381)\cdot(1-P/70.018)\cdot P\) (degree 3),
  2) a **quadratic polynomial in \(P\)**: \(0.1387\cdot(1-P/70.018)\cdot P\) (degree 2),
  3) a **logistic-type rational term**: \(0.1387\cdot \dfrac{P}{1+\exp(-8.0381(P-0.5894))}\).
- Therefore, any matching candidate must be able (after parameter choice) to produce **(polynomial up to degree 3) + (logistic in \(P\) multiplied by \(P\))**, with **no \(|P|\)**, no \(\sin\), no \(\log\), no \(\tanh\), no \(\max\), no \(1/P^k\), etc., unless those parts can be eliminated and the remaining structure still matches.

### 1. \(c0\sin(c1 t+c2)+c3\sin(c4\log(c5 e^{Pc6}+1)+c7)\)
Has \(\sin\) of \(t\) and \(\sin(\log(1+e^{\alpha P}))\). GT has neither sine nor \(\log(1+e^{\cdot})\). You can zero out sine terms only by setting amplitudes \(c0=0\) and \(c3=0\), yielding 0, not GT. **No match.**

### 3. \(Pc0 + P c1/(c2+|P|)+ c3 t/(c4+t)+ c5\sin(\cdots)\)

## GT Analysis

The GT is:
```
0.13870625668024555*(-1 + P/8.038138014396704)*(1 - P/70.01799944958296)*P + 0.13870625668024555*(1 - P/70.01799944958296)*P + 0.13870625668024555*P/(1 + exp(-8.038138014396704*(-0.5894251550796137 + P)))
```

Let me simplify. Let me denote α = 0.13870625668024555, a = 8.038138014396704, b = 70.01799944958296, d = 0.5894251550796137.

**Term 1:** α*(-1 + P/a)*(1 - P/b)*P
**Term 2:** α*(1 - P/b)*P
**Term 3:** α*P/(1 + exp(-a*(-d + P)))

Let me combine Terms 1 and 2:
α*(1 - P/b)*P * [(-1 + P/a) + 1] = α*(1 - P/b)*P * (P/a)
= α*P²/(a*b) * (b - P) ... wait, let me redo:
= α*(P/a)*(1 - P/b)*P = α*P²/a*(1 - P/b)

So Terms 1+2 = α*P²/a - α*P³/(a*b)

Term 3 = α*P/(1 + exp(-a*(P - d)))

So GT = α*P²/a - α*P³/(a*b) + α*P/(1 + exp(-a*(P - d)))

Key observations about GT:
- **No dependence on t** (the variable t does not appear)
- Contains P³, P², and a sigmoid term in P
- The basis functions are: P³, P², and P·sigmoid(P)

Since GT has no t-dependence, any candidate with t-dependent terms must have those terms zeroed out.

Let me also note: α/a ≈ 0.01726, α/(a*b) ≈ 0.000246.

So GT ≈ 0.01726*P² - 0.000246*P³ + 0.1387*P/(1 + exp(-8.038*(P - 0.5894)))

Now let me check each candidate. For candidates with t-dependence, I need to verify that t-terms can be zeroed.

### Candidate 1:
`c0*sin(c1*t + c2) + c3*sin(c4*log(c5*exp(P*c6) + 1) + c7)`

First term depends on t (sinusoidal in t). Set c0=0 to eliminate.
Second term: sin(c4*log(c5*exp(P*c6) + 1) + c7)

GT requires P³, P², and sigmoid terms. A sin(log(exp)) structure cannot produce polynomial terms in P. **[NO MATCH]**

Candidate 1 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 2:
`P*c0 + P*c1*log(c2/(c3 + Abs(P)) + 1) + c4*t/(c5 + t) + c6*sin(c7*log(c8*Abs(P) + 1) + c9)`

Set c4=0 to kill t-term. For P≥0, Abs(P)=P.
Remaining: P*c0 + P*c1*log(c2/(c3+P) + 1) + c6*sin(c7*log(c8*P + 1) + c9)

This has P*linear, P*log(...), and sin(log(...)). No P² or P³ terms, no sigmoid. The log and sin terms cannot produce cubic/quadratic polynomials. **[NO MATCH]**

Candidate 2 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 3:
`P*c0 + P*c1/(c2 + Abs(P)) + c3*t/(c4 + t) + c5*sin(c6*log(c7*Abs(P) + 1) + c8)`

Set c3=0. For P≥0: P*c0 + P*c1/(c2+P) + c5*sin(c6*log(c7*P+1)+c8)

P*c1/(c2+P) is a rational function, sin(log) is oscillatory. Cannot produce P² or P³ or sigmoid. **[NO MATCH]**

Candidate 3 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 4:
`P**2*c0 + P*c1/(c2 + t**2) + P*c3*t**2/(c2 + t**2) + P*c4 + P*c5*exp(P*c6) + P*c7/(P*c8 + 1) + c9*t/(c2 + t**2)`

For t-independence: P*c1/(c2+t²) + P*c3*t²/(c2+t²) + c9*t/(c2+t²) must be t-independent.

P*c1/(c2+t²) + P*c3*t²/(c2+t²) = P*(c1 + c3*t²)/(c2+t²). For this to be t-independent, need c1/1 = c3 (when c2=1), giving P*c3. And c9*t/(c2+t²) must be 0, so c9=0.

So: P²*c0 + P*c3 + P*c4 + P*c5*exp(P*c6) + P*c7/(P*c8+1)

= P²*c0 + P*(c3+c4) + P*c5*exp(P*c6) + P*c7/(P*c8+1)

GT has P³, P², P*sigmoid. 

P*c5*exp(P*c6): This is P*exp(cP), which is NOT a sigmoid. The sigmoid is 1/(1+exp(-aP)).

P*c7/(P*c8+1) is a rational function, not sigmoid.

No P³ term available. **[NO MATCH]**

Candidate 4 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 5:
`P**2*c0 + P*c1 + c2*tanh(c3*t + c4) + c5*log(c6*t + 1)*sin(P*c7 + c8)`

Set c2=0 and c5=0 to kill t-terms. Left with P²*c0 + P*c1. Missing P³ and sigmoid. **[NO MATCH]**

Candidate 5 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 6:

### Candidate 10:

Set c1=0. For P≥0:
P*c0/(P+1) + c3*sin(c4*log(c5*P+1)+c6) + c7*log(c8*exp(P*c9)+1)

The last term c7*log(c8*exp(Pc9)+1) is a softplus-like function. For large P, this ≈ c7*(ln(c8)+Pc9), approximately linear. For small P, it's log(c8+1). This is NOT equivalent to P*sigmoid or P² or P³.

GT needs P³ + P² + P*sigmoid. This candidate has rational P/(P+1), sin(log), and softplus. These are fundamentally different basis functions. **[NO MATCH]**

= [P*c0*t + P*c2 + c3*sin(...) + c7*t + c8*t*sin(...)] / (c1+t)

`P*c0 + P*c1*Max(0, P*c2 - 1) + c3*t/(c4 + t) + c5*sin(c6*log(c7*Abs(P) + 1) + c8)/(c4 + t) + c9*t*sin(c6*log(c7*Abs(P) + 1) + c8)/(c4 + t)`

For this to be constant, need c9/1 = constant and c5 = c9*c4, giving c9. So sin term becomes c9*sin(...). And c3*t/(c4+t) remains t-dependent unless c3=0.

Wait, let me reconsider. (c5+c9*t)/(c4+t) = c9 + (c5-c9*c4)/(c4+t). For t-independence, need c5 = c9*c4. Then it equals c9.

And c3*t/(c4+t) is still t-dependent. Set c3=0.

Remaining: P*c0 + P*c1*Max(0, P*c2-1) + c9*sin(c6*log(c7*P+1)+c8)

### Candidate 44:
`c0*t/(c1 + t**2) + c2*Max(0, P + c3) + c4*exp(c5*t)/(c1 + t**2) + c6*t**2*exp(c5*t)/(c1 + t**2) + c7*t**c8*log(P*c9 + 1)`

For t-independence: set c0=0, c5=0 → c4/(c1+t²) + c6*t²/(c1+t²) = (c4+c6*t²)/(c1+t²). For constant: c4/c1=c6 → constant c6. And c7*t^c8*log(c9*P+1): set c8=0 → c7*log(c9*P+1).
Remaining: c6 + c2*Max(0,P+c3) + c7*log(c9*P+1).
For P≥0, c3≥0: c2*(P+c3) + c7*log(c9*P+1) + c6 = c2*P + c2*c3 + c6 + c7*log(c9*P+1).
Linear + log. No P², P³, sigmoid. **[NO MATCH]**

Candidate 44 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 45:
`P**2*c0 + P*c1 + P*c2 + P*c3/(P + c4) + c5*t + c6*tanh(c7*t + c8) + c9`

Set c5=0, c7=0. P²*c0 + P*(c1+c2) + c3*P/(P+c4) + c6*tanh(c8) + c9.
= P²*c0 + P*(c1+c2) + c3*P/(P+c4) + const.
No P³, no sigmoid. **[NO MATCH]**

Candidate 45 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 46:
`P*c0 + c1*t/(c2 + t**2) + c3*Max(0, P + c4) + c5*exp(c6*t)/(c2 + t**2) + c7*t**2*exp(c6*t)/(c2 + t**2)`

Set c6=0, c1=0: c5/(c2+t²) + c7*t²/(c2+t²) = (c5+c7*t²)/(c2+t²). Constant if c5/c2=c7.
Remaining: P*c0 + c3*Max(0,P+c4) + const. Linear/piecewise linear. No P², P³, sigmoid. **[NO MATCH]**

Candidate 46 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 47:
`P**2*c0 + P*c1 + P*c2*log(c3/(P + c4) + 1) + P**c5*c6 + c7*t**2 + c8*t + c9`

Set c7=0, c8=0. P²*c0 + P*c1 + P*c2*log(c3/(P+c4)+1) + c6*P^c5 + c9.
Set c5=3: P³*c6. Then: P³*c6 + P²*c0 + P*c1 + P*c2*log((c3+P+c4)/(P+c4)) + c9.

The log term is P*log(1+c3/(P+c4)). For large P this ≈ c2*c3*P/(P+c4) → c2*c3. This is NOT zero and NOT equivalent to sigmoid. The GT sigmoid term α*P/(1+exp(-a(P-d))) transitions from ~0 to ~α*P. The log term here has completely different behavior. **[NO MATCH]**

Candidate 47 verdict: [NO MATCH]

Set c3=3: cubic polynomial + constant. No sigmoid. **[NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 50:

Candidate 50 verdict: [NO MATCH]

## Summary

The GT expression contains three fundamentally different basis functions:
1. P³ (cubic polynomial)
2. P² (quadratic polynomial)  
3. P/(1+exp(-a(P-d))) (P times a sigmoid)

None of the candidates contain a sigmoid function (1/(1+exp(...))) or any function that can be algebraically transformed into one. The closest attempts use rational functions P/(P+c), sin(log(...)), tanh(t), exp(P), Max/ReLU, or log functions — none of which are equivalent to a sigmoid.
